31 class InvalidSyntax (Exception):
32     def __init__ (self):

35 # class for represent a token
36 class Token():
37     def __init__ (self, token, t):
38         self.token = token
39         self.t = t

47 def loadFile(fileName):
48     """
49         loadFile: This function loads the file and reads its lines.
50     """
51     global lines
52     fo = open(fileName)
53     for line in fo:
54         lines.append(line)
55     fo.close()

58 def scanner(string):
59     """
60         scanner: This function builds the tokens by the content of the file.
61         The tokens will be saved in list 'tokens'
62     """
63     global tokens
64     token = ""
65     state = 0 # init state
66 
67     for ch in string:
68 
69         if state == 0:
70 
71             if ch == 'm':   # catch mov-command
72 
73                 state = 1
74                 token += 'm'
75 
76             elif ch == 'e': # catch register
77 
78                 state = 4
79                 token += 'e'
80 
81             elif (ch >= '1' and ch <= '9') or ch == '-':    # catch a number
82 
83                 state = 6
84                 token += ch
85 
86             elif ch == '0': # catch a number or hex-code
87 
88                 state = 17
89                 token += ch
90 
91             elif ch == 'a': # catch add-command
92 
93                 state = 7
94                 token += ch
95 
96             elif ch == 's': # catch sub command
97 
98                 state = 10
99                 token += ch
100 
101             elif ch == 'i': # capture int command
102 
103                 state = 14
104                 token += ch
105 
106             elif ch == 'p': # capture push or pop command
107 
108                 state = 19
109                 token += ch
110 
111             elif ch == 'l': # capture label
112 
113                 state = 25
114                 token += ch
115 
116             elif ch == 'j': # capture jmp command
117 
118                 state = 26
119                 token += ch
120 
121             elif ch == 'c': # catch cmp-command
122 
123                 state = 29
124                 token += ch
125 
126             elif ch == ';': # capture comment 
127 
128                 state = 33
129 
130             
131             elif ch == '"': # catch a string
132 
133                 state = 34
134                 # without "
135 
136             elif ch.isupper(): # capture identifier
137 
138                 state = 35
139                 token += ch
140 
141             elif ch == 'd': # capture db keyword
142 
143                 state = 36
144                 token += ch
145 
146             elif ch == "$": # catch variable with prefix $
147 
148                 state = 38
149                 # not catching $
150 
151             elif ch == '_': # catch label for subprogram
152 
153                 state = 40
154                 # not catch the character _
155 
156             elif ch == 'r': # catch ret-command
157 
158                 state = 44
159                 token += ch
160                 
161             else:   # other characters like space-characters etc.
162 
163                 state = 0
164                 token = ""
165         
166         elif state == 1:    # state 1
167 
168             if ch == 'o':
169 
170                 state = 2
171                 token += ch
172 
173             elif ch == 'u':
174 
175                 state = 47
176                 token += ch
177 
178             else: # error case
179 
180                 state = 0
181                 token = ""
182                 raise InvalidSyntax()
183 
184         elif state == 2: # state 2
185 
186             if ch == 'v':
187 
188                 state = 3
189                 token += 'v'
190 
191             else: # error case
192                 state = 0
193                 token = ""
194                 raise InvalidSyntax()
195 
196         elif state == 3: # state 3
197 
198             if ch.isspace():
199 
200                 state = 0
201                 tokens.append(Token(token,"command"))
202                 token = ""
203 
204             else: # error case
205 
206                 state = 0
207                 token = ""
208                 raise InvalidSyntax()
209 
210         elif state == 4:    # state 4
211             if (ch >= 'a' and ch <= 'd'):
212 
213                 state = 5
214                 token += ch
215 
216             else:   # error case
217 
218                 state = 0
219                 token = ""
220                 raise InvalidSyntax()
221 
222         elif state == 5:    # state 5
223             if ch == 'x':
224                 state = 13
225                 token += ch
226             
227             else:   # error case
228 
229                 state = 0
230                 token = ""
231                 raise InvalidSyntax()
232 
233         elif state == 6:    # state 6
234 
235             if ch.isdigit():
236 
237                 state = 6
238                 token += ch
239 
240             elif ch.isspace():
241 
242                 state = 0
243                 tokens.append(Token(token,"value"))
244                 token = ""
245 
246             else:   # error case
247 
248                 state = 0
249                 token = ""
250                 raise InvalidSyntax()
251 
252         elif state == 7:    # state 7
253

920 def scan():
921     """
922         scan: applys function scanner() to each line of the source code.
923     """
924     global lines
925     assert len(lines) > 0 , "no lines"
926     for line in lines:
927         try:
928             scanner(line)
929         except InvalidSyntax:
930             print "line=",line
931     
932 def parser():
933     """
934         parser: parses the tokens of the list 'tokens'
935     """
936 
937     global tokens
938     global eax,ebx,ecx,edx
939 
940     assert len(tokens) > 0 , "no tokens"
941 
942     pointer = 0 # pointer for tokens
943     token = Token("","")
944     tmpToken = Token("","")
945 
946     while pointer < len(tokens):
947 
948         token = tokens[pointer]
949 
950         if token.token == "mov":      # mov commando
951 
952             # it must follow a register
953             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
954                 pointer += 1
955                 token = tokens[pointer]
956             else:
957                 print "Error: Not found argument!"
958                 return
959 
960             # TODO use token.t for this stuff
961             if token.t == "register":
962 
963                 tmpToken = token
964 
965                 # it must follow a value / string / register / variable
966                 if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
967                     pointer += 1
968                     token = tokens[pointer]
969                 else:
970                     print "Error: Not found argument!"
971                     return
972 
973                 # converts the token into float, if token contains olny digits.
974                 # TODO response of float
975                 if token.t == "identifier":     # for variables
976 
977                     # check of exists of variable
978                     if token.token in variables:
979                         token.token = variables[token.token]
980                     else:
981                         print "Error: undefine variable! --> " + token.token
982                         return
983                 elif token.t == "string":
984                     pass
985                 elif isinstance(token.token, float):
986                     pass
987                 elif token.token.isdigit():
988                     token.token = float(token.token)
989                 elif token.token[0] == '-' and token.token[1:].isdigit():
990                     token.token = float(token.token[1:])
991                     token.token *= -1
992                 elif token.t == "register": # loads out of register
993                     if token.token == "eax":
994                         token.token = eax
995                     elif token.token == "ebx":
996                         token.token = ebx
997                     elif token.token == "ecx":
998                         token.token = ecx
999                     elif token.token == "edx":
1000                         token.token = edx
1001 
1002 
1003 
1004                 if tmpToken.token == "eax":
1005                     eax = token.token
1006                 elif tmpToken.token == "ebx":
1007                     ebx = token.token
1008                 elif tmpToken.token == "ecx":
1009                     ecx = token.token
1010                 elif tmpToken.token == "edx":
1011                     edx = token.token
1012 
1013             else:
1014 
1015                 print "Error: No found register!"
1016                 return
1017 
1018         elif token.token == "add":    # add commando
1019 
1020             pointer += 1
1021             token = tokens[pointer]
1022 
1023             if token.t == "register":
1024 
1025                 tmpToken = token
1026 
1027                 if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1028                     pointer += 1
1029                     token = tokens[pointer]
1030                 else:
1031                     print "Error: Not found number!"
1032                     return
1033 
1034 
1035                 # converts the token into float, if token contains olny digits.
1036                 if token.t == "register":
1037                     
1038                     # for the case that token is register
1039                     if token.token == "eax":
1040                         token.token = eax
1041                     elif token.token == "ebx":
1042                         token.token = ebx
1043                     elif token.token == "ecx":
1044                         token.token = ecx
1045                     elif token.token == "edx":
1046                         token.token = edx
1047 
1048                 elif token.token.isdigit():
1049                     token.token = float(token.token)
1050                 elif token.token[0] == '-' and token.token[1:].isdigit():
1051                     token.token = float(token.token[1:])
1052                     token.token *= -1
1053                 else:
1054                     print "Error: ", token," is not a number!"
1055                     return
1056 
1057 
1058 
1059                 if tmpToken.token == "eax":
1060                     eax += token.token
1061 
1062                     # update zero flag
1063                     if eax == 0:
1064                         zeroFlag = True
1065                     else:
1066                         zeroFlag = False
1067                 elif tmpToken.token == "ebx":
1068                     ebx += token.token
1069 
1070                     # update zero flag
1071                     if ebx == 0:
1072                         zeroFlag = True
1073                     else:
1074                         zeroFlag = False
1075                 elif tmpToken.token == "ecx":
1076                     ecx += token.token
1077 
1078                     # update zero flag
1079                     if ecx == 0:
1080                         zeroFlag = True
1081                     else:
1082                         zeroFlag = False
1083                 elif tmpToken.token == "edx":
1084                     edx += token.token
1085 
1086                     # update zero flag
1087                     if edx == 0:
1088                         zeroFlag = True
1089                     else:
1090                         zeroFlag = False
1091                     
1092 
1093 
1094             else:
1095 
1096                 print "Error: No found register!"
1097                 return
1098 
1099         elif token.token == "sub":  # sub commando
1100 
1101             pointer += 1
1102             token = tokens[pointer]
1103 
1104             if token.t == "register":
1105 
1106                 tmpToken = token
1107 
1108                 if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1109                     pointer += 1
1110                     token = tokens[pointer]
1111                 else:
1112                     print "Error: Not found number!"
1113                     return
1114 
1115                 # converts the token into float, if token contains olny digits.
1116                 if token.t == "register":
1117 
1118                     # for the case that token is register
1119                     if token.token == "eax":
1120                         token.token = eax
1121                     elif token.token == "ebx":
1122                         token.token = ebx
1123                     elif token.token == "ecx":
1124                         token.token = ecx
1125                     elif token.token == "edx":
1126                         token.token = edx
1127                 
1128                 elif isinstance(token.token, float):
1129                     pass
1130                 elif token.token.isdigit():
1131                     token.token = float(token.token)
1132                 elif token.token[0] == '-' and token.token[1:].isdigit():
1133                     token.token = float(token.token[1:])
1134                     token.token *= -1
1135                 else:
1136                     print "Error: ", token.token," is not a number!"
1137                     return
1138 
1139 
1140                 if tmpToken.token == "eax":
1141                     eax -= token.token
1142 
1143                     # update zero flag
1144                     if eax == 0:
1145                         zeroFlag = True
1146                     else:
1147                         zeroFlag = False
1148                 elif tmpToken.token == "ebx":
1149                     ebx -= token.token
1150 
1151                     # update zero flag
1152                     if ebx == 0:
1153                         zeroFlag = True
1154                     else:
1155                         zeroFlag = False
1156                 elif tmpToken.token == "ecx":
1157                     ecx -= token.token
1158

1160                     if ecx == 0:
1161                         zeroFlag = True
1162                     else:
1163                         zeroFlag = False
1164                 elif tmpToken.token == "edx":
1165                     edx -= token.token
1166

1168                     if edx == 0:
1169                         zeroFlag = True
1170                     else:
1171                         zeroFlag = False
1172 
1173             else:
1174

1176                 return

1179

1181 
1182             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1183                 pointer += 1
1184                 token = tokens[pointer]
1185             else:

1187                 return

1194                         print "END PROGRAM"
1195                         return

1198                         return
1199

1201

1203 
1204                 elif eax == 4: # output informations
1205

1207 
1208

1210

1212 
1213             # it must follow a register
1214             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1215                 pointer += 1
1216                 token = tokens[pointer]

1219                 return

1222             if token.token == "eax":
1223

1244             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):

1246                 token = tokens[pointer]

1265

1269

1273

1275             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1276                 pointer += 1
1277                 token = tokens[pointer]
1278             else:
1279                 print "Error: Not found label!"
1280                 return
1281 
1282             if token.t == "label":
1283

1287                 print "Error: expected a label!"

1299                 return

1448             else:

1451 
1452             # check of label
1453             if token.t == "label":
1454 
1455                 # actual jump
1456                 if zeroFlag:
1457 
1458                     pointer = jumps[token.token]

1463                  return

1466         elif token.t == "identifier":
1467 
1468             # check whether identifier is in variables-table
1469             if token.token not in variables:
1470 
1471                 # it must follow a command
1472                 if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1473                     pointer += 1
1474                     tmpToken = tokens[pointer] # next register
1475                 else:
1476                     print "Error: Not found argument"
1477                     return
1478 
1479                 if tmpToken.t == "command" and tmpToken.token == "db":
1480 
1481                     # it must follow a value (string)
1482                     if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1483                         pointer += 1
1484                         tmpToken = tokens[pointer] # next register
1485                     else:
1486                         print "Error: Not found argument"
1487                         return
1488 
1489                     if tmpToken.t == "value" or tmpToken.t == "string":
1490 
1491                         if tmpToken.t == "value":
1492                             variables[token.token] = float(tmpToken.token)
1493                         elif tmpToken.t == "string":
1494                             variables[token.token] = tmpToken.token
1495                 
1496 
1497                 else:
1498 
1499                     print "Error: Not found db-keyword"
1500                     return
1501 
1502         elif token.token == "call":     # catch the call-command
1503 
1504             # it must follow a subprogram label
1505             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1506                 pointer += 1
1507                 token = tokens[pointer] # next register
1508             else:
1509                 print "Error: Not found subprogram label"
1510                 return
1511 
1512 
1513             if token.t == "subprogram":
1514 
1515                 if token.token in jumps:
1516 
1517                     # save the current pointer
1518                     returnStack.append(pointer)   # eventuell pointer + 1
1519                     # jump to the subprogram
1520                     pointer = jumps[token.token]
1521                 
1522                 else: # error case
1523 
1524                     print "Error: Unknow subprogram!"
1525                     return
1526 
1527             else:   # error case
1528 
1529                 print "Error: Not found subprogram"
1530                 return
1531 
1532         
1533         elif token.token == "ret":  # catch the ret-command
1534 
1535             if len(returnStack) >= 1:
1536 
1537                 pointer = returnStack.pop() 
1538 
1539             else: # error case
1540 
1541                 print "Error: No return adress on stack"
1542                 return
1543 
1544         elif token.t == "subprogram":
1545 
1546             pass
1547 
1548         
1549         elif token.token == "mul":      # catch mul-command
1550 
1551             # it must follow a register
1552             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1553                 pointer += 1
1554                 token = tokens[pointer] # next register
1555             else:
1556                 print "Error: Not found argument"
1557                 return
1558 
1559             if token.t == "register":
1560 
1561                 if token.token == "eax":
1562 
1563                     eax *= eax
1564 
1565                 elif token.token == "ebx":
1566 
1567                     eax *= ebx
1568 
1569                 elif token.token == "ecx":
1570 
1571                     eax *= ecx
1572 
1573                 elif token.token == "edx":
1574 
1575                     eax *= edx
1576 
1577             else:
1578

1580                 return
1581 
1582 
1583

1585

1587             if pointer+1 < len(tokens):
1588                 pointer += 1
1589                 token = tokens[pointer] # next register
1590             else:
1591                 print "Error: Not found argument"
1592                 return
1593

1595

1597 
1598                     eax /= eax
1599 
1600                 elif token.token == "ebx":
1601

1603

1623 def registerLabels():
1624     """
1625         This function search for labels / subprogram-labels and register this in the 'jumps' list.
1626     """
1627     for i in range(len(tokens)):
1628         if (tokens[i].t == "label"):
1629             jumps[tokens[i].token] = i
1630         elif tokens[i].t == "subprogram":
1631             jumps[tokens[i].token] = i
1632     
1633 
1634 def resetInterpreter():
1635     """
1636         resets the interpreter mind.
1637     """
1638     global eax, ebx, ecx, edx, zeroFlag, stack
1639     global variables, jumps, lines, tokens, returnStack
1640     eax = 0
1641     ebx = 0
1642     ecx = 0
1643     edx = 0
1644     zeroFlag = False
1645     stack = []
1646     jumps = {}
1647     variables = {}
1648     lines = []
1649     tokens = []
1650     returnStack = []
1651

1653 # def printTokens():
1654 #     for token in tokens:
1655 #         print token.token, " --> ", token.t
1656 
1657 
1658 # main program
1659 def main():
1660     """
1661         reads textfiles from the command-line and interprets them. 
1662     """
1663 
1664     # [1:] because the first argument is the program itself.
1665     for arg in sys.argv[1:]:
1666 
1667         resetInterpreter()  # resets interpreter mind
1668 
1669         try:
1670 
1671             loadFile(arg)
1672             scan()
1673             registerLabels()
1674             parser()
1675 
1676         except:
1677 
1678             print "Error: File %s not found!" % (arg)
1679 
1680         
1681 
1682     
1683     
1684 if __name__ == "__main__":
1685     main()

CountMillionCharacter.py
1 '''Simple million word count program.
2     main idea is Python pairs words
3     with the number of times
4     that number appears in the triple quoted string.
5     Credit to William J. Turkel and Adam Crymble for the word
6     frequency code used below. I just merged the two ideas.
7 '''
8 
9 wordstring = '''SCENE I. Yorkshire. Gaultree Forest.
10 Enter the ARCHBISHOP OF YORK, MOWBRAY, LORD HASTINGS, and others
11 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
12 What is this forest call'd?
13 HASTINGS
14 'Tis Gaultree Forest, an't shall please your grace.
15 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
16 Here stand, my lords; and send discoverers forth
17 To know the numbers of our enemies.
18 HASTINGS
19 We have sent forth already.
20 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
21 'Tis well done.
22 My friends and brethren in these great affairs,
23 I must acquaint you that I have received
24 New-dated letters from Northumberland;
25 Their cold intent, tenor and substance, thus:
26 Here doth he wish his person, with such powers
27 As might hold sortance with his quality,
28 The which he could not levy; whereupon
29 He is retired, to ripe his growing fortunes,
30 To Scotland: and concludes in hearty prayers
31 That your attempts may overlive the hazard
32 And fearful melting of their opposite.
33 MOWBRAY
34 Thus do the hopes we have in him touch ground
35 And dash themselves to pieces.
36 Enter a Messenger
37 HASTINGS
38 Now, what news?
39 Messenger
40 West of this forest, scarcely off a mile,
41 In goodly form comes on the enemy;
42 And, by the ground they hide, I judge their number
43 Upon or near the rate of thirty thousand.
44 MOWBRAY
45 The just proportion that we gave them out
46 Let us sway on and face them in the field.
47 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
48 What well-appointed leader fronts us here?
49 Enter WESTMORELAND
50 MOWBRAY
51 I think it is my Lord of Westmoreland.
52 WESTMORELAND
53 Health and fair greeting from our general,
54 The prince, Lord John and Duke of Lancaster.
55 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
56 Say on, my Lord of Westmoreland, in peace:
57 What doth concern your coming?
58 WESTMORELAND
59 Then, my lord,
60 Unto your grace do I in chief address
61 The substance of my speech. If that rebellion
62 Came like itself, in base and abject routs,
63 Led on by bloody youth, guarded with rags,
64 And countenanced by boys and beggary,
65 I say, if damn'd commotion so appear'd,
66 In his true, native and most proper shape,
67 You, reverend father, and these noble lords
68 Had not been here, to dress the ugly form
69 Of base and bloody insurrection
70 With your fair honours. You, lord archbishop,
71 Whose see is by a civil peace maintained,
72 Whose beard the silver hand of peace hath touch'd,
73 Whose learning and good letters peace hath tutor'd,
74 Whose white investments figure innocence,
75 The dove and very blessed spirit of peace,
76 Wherefore do you so ill translate ourself
77 Out of the speech of peace that bears such grace,
78 Into the harsh and boisterous tongue of war;
79 Turning your books to graves, your ink to blood,
80 Your pens to lances and your tongue divine
81 To a trumpet and a point of war?
82 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
83 Wherefore do I this? so the question stands.
84 Briefly to this end: we are all diseased,
85 And with our surfeiting and wanton hours
86 Have brought ourselves into a burning fever,
87 And we must bleed for it; of which disease
88 Our late king, Richard, being infected, died.
89 But, my most noble Lord of Westmoreland,
90 I take not on me here as a physician,
91 Nor do I as an enemy to peace
92 Troop in the throngs of military men;
93 But rather show awhile like fearful war,
94 To diet rank minds sick of happiness
95 And purge the obstructions which begin to stop
96 Our very veins of life. Hear me more plainly.
97 I have in equal balance justly weigh'd
98 What wrongs our arms may do, what wrongs we suffer,
99 And find our griefs heavier than our offences.
100 We see which way the stream of time doth run,
101 And are enforced from our most quiet there
102 By the rough torrent of occasion;
103 And have the summary of all our griefs,
104 When time shall serve, to show in articles;
105 Which long ere this we offer'd to the king,
106 And might by no suit gain our audience:
107 When we are wrong'd and would unfold our griefs,
108 We are denied access unto his person
109 Even by those men that most have done us wrong.
110 The dangers of the days but newly gone,
111 Whose memory is written on the earth
112 With yet appearing blood, and the examples
113 Of every minute's instance, present now,
114 Hath put us in these ill-beseeming arms,
115 Not to break peace or any branch of it,
116 But to establish here a peace indeed,
117 Concurring both in name and quality.
118 WESTMORELAND
119 When ever yet was your appeal denied?
120 Wherein have you been galled by the king?
121 What peer hath been suborn'd to grate on you,
122 That you should seal this lawless bloody book
123 Of forged rebellion with a seal divine
124 And consecrate commotion's bitter edge?
125 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
126 My brother general, the commonwealth,
127 To brother born an household cruelty,
128 I make my quarrel in particular.
129 WESTMORELAND
130 There is no need of any such redress;
131 Or if there were, it not belongs to you.
132 MOWBRAY
133 Why not to him in part, and to us all
134 That feel the bruises of the days before,
135 And suffer the condition of these times
136 To lay a heavy and unequal hand
137 Upon our honours?
138 WESTMORELAND
139 O, my good Lord Mowbray,
140 Construe the times to their necessities,
141 And you shall say indeed, it is the time,
142 And not the king, that doth you injuries.
143 Yet for your part, it not appears to me
144 Either from the king or in the present time
145 That you should have an inch of any ground
146 To build a grief on: were you not restored
147 To all the Duke of Norfolk's signories,
148 Your noble and right well remember'd father's?
149 MOWBRAY
150 What thing, in honour, had my father lost,
151 That need to be revived and breathed in me?
152 The king that loved him, as the state stood then,
153 Was force perforce compell'd to banish him:
154 And then that Harry Bolingbroke and he,
155 Being mounted and both roused in their seats,
156 Their neighing coursers daring of the spur,
157 Their armed staves in charge, their beavers down,
158 Their eyes of fire sparking through sights of steel
159 And the loud trumpet blowing them together,
160 Then, then, when there was nothing could have stay'd
161 My father from the breast of Bolingbroke,
162 O when the king did throw his warder down,
163 His own life hung upon the staff he threw;
164 Then threw he down himself and all their lives
165 That by indictment and by dint of sword
166 Have since miscarried under Bolingbroke.
167 WESTMORELAND
168 You speak, Lord Mowbray, now you know not what.
169 The Earl of Hereford was reputed then
170 In England the most valiant gentlemen:
171 Who knows on whom fortune would then have smiled?
172 But if your father had been victor there,
173 He ne'er had borne it out of Coventry:
174 For all the country in a general voice
175 Cried hate upon him; and all their prayers and love
176 Were set on Hereford, whom they doted on
177 And bless'd and graced indeed, more than the king.
178 But this is mere digression from my purpose.
179 Here come I from our princely general
180 To know your griefs; to tell you from his grace
181 That he will give you audience; and wherein
182 It shall appear that your demands are just,
183 You shall enjoy them, every thing set off
184 That might so much as think you enemies.
185 MOWBRAY
186 But he hath forced us to compel this offer;
187 And it proceeds from policy, not love.
188 WESTMORELAND
189 Mowbray, you overween to take it so;
190 This offer comes from mercy, not from fear:
191 For, lo! within a ken our army lies,
192 Upon mine honour, all too confident
193 To give admittance to a thought of fear.
194 Our battle is more full of names than yours,
195 Our men more perfect in the use of arms,
196 Our armour all as strong, our cause the best;
197 Then reason will our heart should be as good
198 Say you not then our offer is compell'd.
199 MOWBRAY
200 Well, by my will we shall admit no parley.
201 WESTMORELAND
202 That argues but the shame of your offence:
203 A rotten case abides no handling.
204 HASTINGS
205 Hath the Prince John a full commission,
206 In very ample virtue of his father,
207 To hear and absolutely to determine
208 Of what conditions we shall stand upon?
209 WESTMORELAND
210 That is intended in the general's name:
211 I muse you make so slight a question.
212 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
213 Then take, my Lord of Westmoreland, this schedule,
214 For this contains our general grievances:
215 Each several article herein redress'd,
216 All members of our cause, both here and hence,
217 That are insinew'd to this action,
218 Acquitted by a true substantial form
219 And present execution of our wills
220 To us and to our purposes confined,
221 We come within our awful banks again
222 And knit our powers to the arm of peace.
223 WESTMORELAND
224 This will I show the general. Please you, lords,
225 In sight of both our battles we may meet;
226 And either end in peace, which God so frame!
227 Or to the place of difference call the swords
228 Which must decide it.
229 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
230 My lord, we will do so.
231 Exit WESTMORELAND
232 MOWBRAY
233 There is a thing within my bosom tells me
234 That no conditions of our peace can stand.
235 HASTINGS
236 Fear you not that: if we can make our peace
237 Upon such large terms and so absolute
238 As our conditions shall consist upon,
239 Our peace shall stand as firm as rocky mountains.
240 MOWBRAY
241 Yea, but our valuation shall be such
242 That every slight and false-derived cause,
243 Yea, every idle, nice and wanton reason
244 Shall to the king taste of this action;
245 That, were our royal faiths martyrs in love,
246 We shall be winnow'd with so rough a wind
247 That even our corn shall seem as light as chaff
248 And good from bad find no partition.
249 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
250 No, no, my lord. Note this;    the king is weary
251 Of dainty and such picking grievances:
252 For he hath found to end one doubt by death
253 Revives two greater in the heirs of life,
254 And therefore will he wipe his tables clean
255 And keep no tell-tale to his memory
256 That may repeat and history his loss
257 To new remembrance; for full well he knows
258 He cannot so precisely weed this land
259 As his misdoubts present occasion:
260 His foes are so enrooted with his friends
261 That, plucking to unfix an enemy,
262 He doth unfasten so and shake a friend:
263 So that this land, like an offensive wife
264 That hath enraged him on to offer strokes,
265 As he is striking, holds his infant up
266 And hangs resolved correction in the arm
267 That was uprear'd to execution.
268 HASTINGS
269 Besides, the king hath wasted all his rods
270 On late offenders, that he now doth lack
271 The very instruments of chastisement:
272 So that his power, like to a fangless lion,
273 May offer, but not hold.
274 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
275 'Tis very true:
276 And therefore be assured, my good lord marshal,
277 If we do now make our atonement well,
278 Our peace will, like a broken limb united,
279 Grow stronger for the breaking.
280 MOWBRAY
281 Be it so.
282 Here is return'd my Lord of Westmoreland.
283 Re-enter WESTMORELAND
284 WESTMORELAND
285 The prince is here at hand: pleaseth your lordship
286 To meet his grace just distance 'tween our armies.
287 MOWBRAY
288 Your grace of York, in God's name then, set forward.
289 ARCHBISHOP OF YORK
290 Before, and greet his grace: my lord, we come.
291 Exeunt'''
292 
293 wordlist = wordstring.split()
294 
295 wordfreq = [wordlist.count(w) for w in wordlist]
296 
297 print("String\n {} \n".format(wordstring))
298 print("List\n {} \n".format(str(wordlist)))
299 print("Frequencies\n {} \n".format(str(wordfreq)))
300 print("Pairs\n {}".format(str(dict(zip(wordlist, wordfreq)))))

CountMillionCharacters-2.0.py

2 """Get the number of each character in any given text.
3 Inputs:
4 A txt file -- You will be asked for an input file. Simply input the name
5 of the txt file in which you have the desired text.
6 """
7 
8 import pprint
9 import collections
10 
11 
12 def main():
13 
14     file_input = input('File Name: ')
15     try:
16         with open(file_input, 'r') as info:
17             count = collections.Counter(info.read().upper())
18     except FileNotFoundError:
19         print("Please enter a valid file name.")
20         main()
21 
22     value = pprint.pformat(count)
23     print(value)
24     exit()
25 
26 
27 if __name__ == "__main__":
28     main()

9 def count_chars(filename):
10     count = {}
11 
12     with open(filename) as info:  # inputFile Replaced with filename
13         readfile = info.read()
14         for character in readfile.upper():
15             count[character] = count.get(character, 0) + 1
16 
17     return count

Credit_Card_Validator.py
1 #luhn algorithm
2 
3 class CreditCard:
4     def __init__(self,card_no):
5         self.card_no = card_no
6 
7 
8     @property
9     def company(self):
10         comp =None
11         if str(self.card_no).startswith('4'):
12              comp = 'Visa Card'
13         elif str(self.card_no).startswith(('50', '67', '58','63',)):
14             comp = 'Maestro Card'
15         elif str(self.card_no).startswith('5'):
16             comp = 'Master Card'
17         elif str(self.card_no).startswith('37'):
18             comp = 'American Express Card'
19         elif str(self.card_no).startswith('62'):
20             comp = 'Unionpay Card'
21         elif str(self.card_no).startswith('6'):
22             comp = 'Discover Card'
23         elif str(self.card_no).startswith('35'):
24             comp = 'JCB Card'
25         elif str(self.card_no).startswith('7'):
26             comp = 'Gasoline Card'
27 
28         return 'Company : '+comp
29 
30 
31 
32     def first_check(self):
33         if 13<=len(self.card_no)<=19:
34             message = "First check : Valid in terms of length."
35 
36         else:
37             message = "First chek : Check Card number once again it must be of 13 or 16 digit long."
38         return message
39 
40 
41 
42 
43     def validate(self):
44         #double every second digit from right to left
45         sum_=0
46         crd_no = self.card_no[::-1]
47         for i in range(len(crd_no)):
48             if i%2==1:
49                 double_it = int(crd_no[i])*2
50 
51                 if len(str(double_it))==2:
52                     sum_ += sum([eval(i) for i in str(double_it)])
53 
54                 else:
55                     sum_+=double_it
56 
57             else:
58                 sum_+=int(crd_no[i])
59 
60 
61 
62         if sum_%10==0:
63             response = "Valid Card"
64         else:
65             response = 'Invalid Card'
66 
67         return response
68 
69 
70 
71     @property
72     def checksum(self):
73         return '#CHECKSUM# : '+self.card_no[-1]
74 
75 
76     @classmethod
77     def set_card(cls,card_to_check):
78         return cls(card_to_check)
79 
80 
81 
82 card_number  = input()
83 card = CreditCard.set_card(card_number)
84 print(card.company)
85 print('Card : ',card.card_no)
86 print(card.first_check())
87 print(card.checksum)
88 print(card.validate())
89

93 #4388576018402626
94 #379354508162306

EncryptionTool.py
1 #GGearing
2 #Simple encryption script for text
3 #This was one my first versions of this script
4 #09/07/2017
5 import math
6 
7 text=input("Enter text: ")
8 values= []
9 reverse= []
10 def encryptChar(target):
11     #encrytion algorithm
12     target=(((target+42)*math.pi)-449)
13     return target
14 
15 def decryptChar(target):
16     target=(((target+449)/math.pi)-42)
17     return target
18 
19 def encrypt(input_text):
20     col_values= []
21     for i in range (len(input_text)):
22         current=ord(input_text[i])
23         current=encryptChar(current)
24         col_values.append(current)
25     return col_values
26 
27 def decrypt(enc_text):
28     col_values = []
29     for i in range (len(enc_text)):
30         current=int(decryptChar(enc_text[i]))
31         current=chr(current)
32         col_values.append(current)
33     return col_values
34 
35 def readAndDecrypt(filename):
36     file=open(filename,"r")
37     data=file.read()
38     datalistint= []
39     actualdata= []
40     datalist=data.split(" ")
41     datalist.remove('')
42     for i in range(len(datalist)):
43         datalistint.append(float(datalist[i]))
44     for i in range(len(datalist)):
45         current1=int(decryptChar(datalistint[i]))
46         current1=chr(current1)
47         actualdata.append(current1)
48     file.close()
49     return actualdata
50 
51 def readAndEncrypt(filename):
52     file=open(filename,"r")
53     data=file.read()
54     datalist=list(data)
55     encrypted_list=list()
56     encrypted_list_str=list()
57     for i in range(len(datalist)):
58         current=ord(datalist[i])
59         current=encryptChar(current)
60         encrypted_list.append(current)
61     file.close()
62     return encrypted_list
63 
64 def readAndEncryptAndSave(inp_file,out_file):
65     enc_list=readAndEncrypt(inp_file)
66     output=open(out_file,"w")
67     for i in range(len(enc_list)):
68         output.write(str(enc_list[i])+" ")
69     output.close()
70 
71 def readAndDecryptAndSave(inp_file,out_file):
72     dec_list=readAndDecrypt(inp_file)
73     output=open(out_file,"w")
74     for i in range(len(dec_list)):
75         output.write(str(dec_list[i]))
76     output.close()
77 
78 #encryption
79 for i in range (len(text)):
80     current=ord(text[i])
81     current=encryptChar(current)
82     values.append(current)
83 
84 #decryption
85 for i in range (len(text)):
86     current=int(decryptChar(values[i]))
87     current=chr(current)
88     reverse.append(current)
89 print(reverse)
90 
91 #saves encrypted in txt file
92 output=open("encrypted.txt","w")
93 for i in range(len(values)):
94     output.write(str(values[i])+" ")
95 output.close()
96 
97 #read and decrypts
98 print(readAndDecrypt("encrypted.txt"))

FTP in python
1  How to use FTP in Python
2 Overview
3 This article will show how you can use FTP in Python with the help of the
4 ftplib module. 
5 Ftplib
6 The ftplib module in Python allows you to write Python programs that perform a
7 variety of automated FTP jobs. You can easily connect to a FTP server to retrieve
8 files and process them locally.
9 
10 To use the ftplib module in Python, you first have to import it into your script. 
11 Open a Connection
12 To "open" a connection to the FTP Server, you have to create the object.
13 
14 Once the connection is made (opened), you can use the methods in the ftplib
15 module.
16 
17 Several methods are available in two flavors: one for handling text files and
18 another for binary files.
19 
20 You can easily navigate the directory structure, manage and download files. 
21 How do I use it?
22 This program will first connect to a FTP server (ftp.cwi.nl) and then list the
23 files and directories in the FTP server root directory using the LIST() method.
24 from ftplib import FTP
25 
26 ftp = FTP('ftp.cwi.nl')   # connect to host, default port
27 
28 ftp.login()               # user anonymous, passwd anonymous@
29 
30 ftp.retrlines('LIST')     # list directory contents 
31 Our second program opens a connection to 'ftp.sunet.se' as the user 'anonymous'
32 with an email address of 'anonymous@sunet.se'
33 
34 It then lists the files and directories on the FTP server by using the dir()
35 method.
36 
37 The output is saved to the 'files' variable. 
38 
39 I then use print to see the files on screen. 
40 
41 If I want I to change directory I would just use ftp.cwd(path) to do so.
42 
43 To close the FTP connection, use the quit() method.  
44 import ftplib
45 
46 ftp = ftplib.FTP('ftp.sunet.se', 'anonymous', 'anonymous@sunet.se')
47 
48 print "File List: "
49 
50 files = ftp.dir()
51 
52 print files
53 
54 ftp.cwd("/pub/unix") #changing to /pub/unix
55 Common FTP Methods
56 FTP.connect(host[, port[, timeout]])
57 
58 Connect to the given host and port. 
59 
60 The default port number is 21, as specified by the FTP protocol specification. 
61 
62 It is rarely needed to specify a different port number. 
63 
64 This function should be called only once for each instance 
65 
66 It should not be called at all if a host was given when the instance was created. 
67 
68 All other methods can only be used after a connection
69 has been made.
70 
71 The optional timeout parameter specifies a timeout in seconds for the connection
72 attempt. 
73 
74 If no timeout is passed, the global default timeout setting will be used.
75 FTP.getwelcome()
76 
77 Return the welcome message sent by the server in reply to the initial connection. 
78 
79 This message sometimes contains disclaimers or help information that may be
80 relevant to the user
81 FTP.login([user[, passwd[, acct]]])
82 
83 Log in as the given user. 
84 
85 The passwd and acct parameters are optional and default to the empty string. 
86 
87 If no user is specified, it defaults to 'anonymous'. 
88 
89 If user is 'anonymous', the default passwd is 'anonymous@'. 
90 
91 This function should be called only once for each instance, after a connection 
92 has been established. 
93 
94 It should not be called at all if a host and user were given when the instance
95 was created. 
96 
97 Most FTP commands are only allowed after the client has logged in. 
98 
99 The acct parameter supplies “accounting information”; few systems implement this.
100 FTP.retrbinary(command, callback[, maxblocksize[, rest]])
101 
102 
103  
104 Retrieve a file in binary transfer mode. 
105 
106 Command should be an appropriate RETR command: 'RETR filename'. 
107 
108 The callback function is called for each block of data received, with a single
109 string argument giving the data block. 
110 
111 The optional maxblocksize argument specifies the maximum chunk size to read on
112 the low-level socket object created to do the actual transfer.
113 
114 A reasonable default is chosen. rest means the same thing as in the transfercmd()
115 method.
116 FTP.retrlines(command[, callback])
117 
118 Retrieve a file or directory listing in ASCII transfer mode. 
119 
120 Command should be an appropriate RETR command or a command such as LIST, NLST or 
121 MLSD.
122 
123 LIST retrieves a list of files and information about those files. 
124 
125 NLST retrieves a list of file names. 
126 
127 On some servers, MLSD retrieves a machine readable list of files and information
128 about those files. 
129 
130 The callback function is called for each line with a string argument containing
131 the line with the trailing CRLF stripped. 
132 
133 The default callback prints the line to sys.stdout.
134 FTP.dir(argument[, ...])
135 
136 Produce a directory listing as returned by the LIST command, printing it to
137 standard output.
138 
139 The optional argument is a directory to list (default is the current server
140 directory). 
141 
142 Multiple arguments can be used to pass non-standard options to the LIST command. 
143 
144 If the last argument is a function, it is used as a callback function as for 
145 retrlines(); the default prints to sys.stdout. 
146 
147 This method returns None.
148 FTP.delete(filename)
149 
150 Remove the file named filename from the server. 
151 
152 If successful, returns the text of the response, otherwise raises error_perm on 
153 permission errors or error_reply on other errors.
154 FTP.cwd(pathname)
155 
156 Set the current directory on the server.
157 FTP.mkd(pathname)
158 
159 Create a new directory on the server.
160 FTP.pwd()
161 
162 Return the pathname of the current directory on the server.
163 FTP.quit()
164 
165 Send a QUIT command to the server and close the connection. 
166 
167 This is the “polite” way to close a connection, but it may raise an exception if
168 the server responds with an error to the QUIT command. 
169 
170 This implies a call to the close() method which renders the FTP instance useless
171 for subsequent calls.
172 FTP.close()
173 
174 Close the connection unilaterally. 
175 
176 This should not be applied to an already closed connection such as after a 
177 successful call to quit(). 
178 
179 After this call the FTP instance should not be used any more.
180 
181 After a call to close() or quit() you cannot reopen the connection by issuing
182 another login() method).

create_dir.py
1 #!/usr/bin/python3
2 
3 """
4 Code to directly use in file to
5 create directory in home location
6 
7 Note:- I Have used python package so if you want
8 to create in the main directory of your project use
9 pardir+"\\"+name in functions
10 
11 All the folder operations are done on home
12 project directory.
13 """
14 
15 from shutil import copytree
16 from shutil import move
17 from os import chdir
18 from os.path import exists
19 from os.path import pardir
20 from os import makedirs
21 from os import removedirs
22 from os import rename
23 
24 
25 # Creates a directory
26 def create_directory(name):
27     if exists(pardir+"\\"+name):
28         print('Folder already exists... Cannot Overwrite this')
29     else:
30         makedirs(pardir+"\\"+name)
31 
32 
33 # Deletes a directory
34 def delete_directory(name):
35     removedirs(name)
36 
37 
38 # Rename a directory
39 def rename_directory(direct, name):
40     rename(direct, name)
41 
42 
43 # Sets the working directory
44 def set_working_directory():
45     chdir(pardir)
46 
47 
48 # Backup the folder tree
49 def backup_files(name_dir, folder):
50     copytree(pardir, name_dir + ':\\' + folder)
51 
52 
53 # Move folder to specific location
54 # Overwrites the file if it already exists
55 def move_folder(filename, name_dir, folder):
56     if not exists(name_dir+":\\"+folder):
57         makedirs(name_dir+':\\'+folder)
58     move(filename, name_dir+":\\"+folder+'\\')
59 
60 
61 """
62 For test purpose:
63     1. create_directory("test")
64     2. rename_directory("test","demo")
65     3. delete_directory("demo")
66     4. backup_files('D', 'backup_project')
67     5. move_folder(pardir+'\\'+'test.txt', 'D', 'name')
68 """

image grapper.py
1 #!/usr/bin/python3
2 
3 from os import chdir
4 import requests
5 from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
6 from urllib.request import urlopen, Request
7 from urllib.parse import urlencode
8 from os import walk
9 import json
10 from os.path import curdir
11 from urllib.request import urlretrieve
12 from os.path import pardir
13 from create_dir import create_directory
14 
15 GOOGLE_IMAGE = 'https://www.google.com/search?site=&tbm=isch&source=hp&biw=1873&bih=990&'
16 WALLPAPERS_KRAFT = 'https://wallpaperscraft.com/search/keywords?'
17 usr_agent = {
18         'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) AppleWebKit/537.11 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/23.0.1271.64 Safari/537.11',
19         'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8',
20         'Accept-Charset': 'ISO-8859-1,utf-8;q=0.7,*;q=0.3',
21         'Accept-Encoding': 'none',
22         'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.8',
23         'Connection': 'keep-alive'
24         }
25 
26 
27 def image_grabber(ch):
28 
29     # Download images from google images
30     if ch == 1:
31         print('Enter data to download Images: ')
32         data = input()
33         search_query = {'q': data}
34         search = urlencode(search_query)
35         print(search)
36         g = GOOGLE_IMAGE + search
37         request = Request(g, headers=usr_agent)
38         r = urlopen(request).read()
39         sew = BeautifulSoup(r, 'html.parser')
40         images = []
41         # print(sew.prettify())
42         results = sew.findAll("div",{"class":"rg_meta"})
43         for re in results:
44             link, Type = json.loads(re.text)["ou"] , json.loads(re.text)["ity"]
45             images.append(link)
46         counter = 0
47         for re in images:
48             rs = requests.get(re)
49             with open('img' + str(counter) + '.jpg', 'wb') as file:
50                 file.write(rs.content)
51                 # urlretrieve(re, 'img' + str(count) + '.jpg')
52                 counter += 1
53         return True
54 
55     elif ch == 2:
56         cont = set()  # Stores the links of images
57         temp = set()  # Refines the links to download images
58 
59         print('Enter data to download wallpapers: ')
60         data = input()
61         search_query = {'q': data}
62         search = urlencode(search_query)
63         print(search)
64         g = WALLPAPERS_KRAFT + search
65         request = Request(g, headers=usr_agent)
66         r = urlopen(request).read()
67         sew = BeautifulSoup(r, 'html.parser')
68         count = 0
69         for links in sew.find_all('a'):
70             if 'wallpaperscraft.com/download' in links.get('href'):
71                 cont.add(links.get('href'))
72         for re in cont:
73             # print all valid links
74             # print('https://wallpaperscraft.com/image/' + re[31:-10] + '_' + re[-9:] + '.jpg')
75             temp.add('https://wallpaperscraft.com/image/' + re[31:-10] + '_' + re[-9:] + '.jpg')
76 
77         # Goes to Each link and downloads high resolution images
78 
79         for re in temp:
80             rs = requests.get(re)
81             with open('img' + str(count) + '.jpg', 'wb') as file:
82                 file.write(rs.content)
83             # urlretrieve(re, 'img' + str(count) + '.jpg')
84             count += 1
85 
86         return True
87 
88     elif ch == 3:
89         for folders, subfolder, files in walk(curdir):
90             for folder in subfolder:
91                 print(folder)
92         return True
93 
94     elif ch == 4:
95         print('Enter the directory to be set: ')
96         data = input()
97         chdir(data + ':\\')
98         print('Enter name for the folder: ')
99         data = input()
100         create_directory(data)
101         return True
102 
103     elif ch == 5:
104         print(
105                 '''
106 -------------------------***Thank You For Using***-------------------------
107             '''
108             )
109         return False
110 
111 
112 run = True
113 
114 print(
115         '''
116 ***********[First Creating Folder To Save Your Images}***********
117     '''
118     )
119 
120 create_directory('Images')
121 DEFAULT_DIRECTORY = pardir + '\\Images'
122 chdir(DEFAULT_DIRECTORY)
123 
124 while run:
125     print('''
126 -------------------------WELCOME-------------------------
127     1. Search for image
128     2. Download Wallpapers 1080p
129     3. View Images in your directory
130     4. Set directory
131     5. Exit
132 -------------------------*******-------------------------
133     ''')
134     choice = input()
135     run = image_grabber(int(choice))

GroupSms_Way2.py
1 #!/usr/bin/python
2  
3 import urllib2
4 import cookielib
5 from getpass import getpass
6 import sys
7  
8 username = raw_input('Enter mobile number:')
9 passwd = getpass()
10 message = raw_input('Enter Message:')
11 #Fill the list with Recipients
12 x=raw_input('Enter Mobile numbers seperated with comma:')
13 num=x.split(',')
14 message = "+".join(message.split(' '))
15  
16 #Logging into the SMS Site
17 url = 'http://site24.way2sms.com/Login1.action?'
18 data = 'username='+username+'&password='+passwd+'&Submit=Sign+in'
19  
20 #For Cookies:
21 cj = cookielib.CookieJar()
22 opener = urllib2.build_opener(urllib2.HTTPCookieProcessor(cj))
23  
24 # Adding Header detail:
25 opener.addheaders = [('User-Agent','Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/37.0.2062.120 Safari/537.36')]

29 except IOError:

koch curve.py
1 #importing the libraries
2 #turtle standard graphics library for python
3 from turtle import *
4 
5 #function to create koch snowflake or koch curve
6 def snowflake(lengthSide, levels):
7     if levels == 0:
8         forward(lengthSide)
9         return
10     lengthSide /= 3.0
11     snowflake(lengthSide, levels-1)
12     left(60)
13     snowflake(lengthSide, levels-1)
14     right(120)
15     snowflake(lengthSide, levels-1)
16     left(60)
17     snowflake(lengthSide, levels-1)
18 
19 #main function
20 if __name__ == "__main__":
21     speed(0)                    #defining the speed of the turtle
22     length = 300.0              #
23     penup()                     #Pull the pen up – no drawing when moving.
24     #Move the turtle backward by distance, opposite to the direction the turtle is headed.
25     #Do not change the turtle’s heading.
26     backward(length/2.0)
27     pendown()
28     for i in range(3):
29          #Pull the pen down – drawing when moving.
30          snowflake(length, 4)
31          right(120)
32     #To control the closing windows of the turtle
33     mainloop()================
Monitor Apache
1 Monitor Apache / Nginx Log File
2 Count the number of hits in a Apache/Nginx
3 This small script will count the number of hits in a Apache/Nginx log file. 
4 How it works
5 This script can easily be adapted to any other log file. 
6 
7 The script starts with making an empty dictionary for storing the IP addresses andcount how many times they exist. 
8 
9 Then we open the file (in this example the Nginx access.log file) and read the
10 content line by line. 
11 
12 The for loop go through the file and splits the strings to get the IP address. 
13 
14 The len() function is used to ensure the length of IP address. 
15 
16 If the IP already exists , increase by 1.
17 ips = {}
18 
19 fh = open("/var/log/nginx/access.log", "r").readlines()
20 for line in fh:
21     ip = line.split(" ")[0]
22     if 6 < len(ip) <=15:
23         ips[ip] = ips.get(ip, 0) + 1
24 print ips
25 Test it out
26 If you now browse to your website, and run the python script, you should see your IP address + the counts.

1 import os

3 import shutil
4 
5 EXT_VIDEO_LIST = ['FLV', 'WMV', 'MOV', 'MP4', 'MPEG', '3GP', 'MKV','AVI']
6 EXT_IMAGE_LIST = ['JPG', 'JPEG', 'GIF', 'PNG', 'SVG']
7 EXT_DOCUMENT_LIST = ['DOC', 'DOCX', 'PPT', 'PPTX', 'PAGES', 'PDF', 'ODT', 'ODP', 'XLSX', 'XLS', 'ODS', 'TXT', 'IN', 'OUT', 'MD']
8 EXT_MUSIC_LIST = ['MP3', 'WAV', 'WMA', 'MKA', 'AAC', 'MID', 'RA', 'RAM', 'RM', 'OGG']
9 EXT_CODE_LIST = ['CPP', 'RB', 'PY', 'HTML', 'CSS', 'JS']
10 EXT_EXECUTABLE_LIST = ['LNK','DEB', 'EXE', 'SH', 'BUNDLE']
11 EXT_COMPRESSED_LIST = ['RAR', 'JAR', 'ZIP', 'TAR', 'MAR', 'ISO', 'LZ', '7ZIP', 'TGZ', 'GZ', 'BZ2']
12 
13 # Taking the location of the Folder to Arrange
14 try:
15 	destLocation = str(sys.argv[1])
16 except IndexError:
17 	destLocation = str(input('Enter the Path of directory: '))
18 
19 # When we make a folder that already exist then WindowsError happen
20 # Changing directory may give WindowsError
21 def ChangeDirectory(dir):
22 	try:
23 		os.chdir(dir)
24 	except WindowsError:
25 		print ('Error! Cannot change the Directory')
26 		print ('Enter a valid directory!')
27 		ChangeDirectory(str(input('Enter the Path of directory: ')))
28 ChangeDirectory(destLocation)
29 
30 def Organize(dirs, name):
31 	try:
32 		os.mkdir(name)
33 		print ('{} Folder Created'.format(name))
34 	except WindowsError:
35 		print ('{} Folder Exist'.format(name))
36 	
37 	src = '{}\\{}'.format(destLocation, dirs)
38 	dest = '{}\{}'.format(destLocation, name)
39 
40 	os.chdir(dest)
41 	shutil.move(src, '{}\\{}'.format(dest, dirs))
42 
43 	print os.getcwd()
44 	os.chdir(destLocation)
45 
46 TYPES_LIST = ['Video', 'Images', 'Documents', 'Music', 'Codes', 'Executables', 'Compressed']
47 for dirs in os.listdir(os.getcwd()):
48 	if 1:
49 		for name, extensions_list in zip(TYPES_LIST, [EXT_VIDEO_LIST, EXT_IMAGE_LIST, EXT_DOCUMENT_LIST, EXT_MUSIC_LIST, EXT_CODE_LIST, EXT_EXECUTABLE_LIST, EXT_COMPRESSED_LIST]):
50 			if dirs.split('.')[-1].upper() in extensions_list:
51 				Organize(dirs, name)
52 	else:
53 		if dirs not in TYPES_LIST:
54 			Organize(dirs, 'Folders')
55 
56 print ('Done Arranging Files and Folder in your specified directory')

QuadraticCalc.py
1 #GGearing
2 #02/10/2017
3 #Simple script to calculate the quadratic formula of a sequence of numbers and
4 #recognises when the sequence isn't quadratic
5 
6 def findLinear(numbers):    ##find a & b of linear sequence
7     output=[]
8     a=numbers[1]-numbers[0]
9     a1=numbers[2]-numbers[1]
10     if a1==a:
11         b=numbers[0]-a
12         return (a,b)
13     else:
14         print("Sequence is not linear")
15         
16 sequence=[]
17 first_difference=[]
18 second_difference=[]
19 for i in range(4):  #input
20     term=str(i+1)
21     inp=int(input("Enter term "+term+": "))
22     sequence.append(inp)
23     
24 for i in range(3):
25     gradient=sequence[i+1]-sequence[i]
26     first_difference.append(gradient)
27 for i in range(2):
28     gradient=first_difference[i+1]-first_difference[i]
29     second_difference.append(gradient)
30     
31 if second_difference[0]==second_difference[1]:  #checks to see if consistent
32     a=second_difference[0]/2
33     subs_diff=[]
34     for i in range(4):
35         n=i+1
36         num=a*(n*n)
37         subs_diff.append((sequence[i])-num)
38     b,c=findLinear(subs_diff)
39     print("Nth term: "+str(a)+"n^2 + "+str(b)+"n + "+str(c)) #outputs nth term
40 else:
41     print("Sequence is not quadratic")
42

SimpleStopWatch.py
1 #Author: OMKAR PATHAK
2 #This script helps to build a simple stopwatch application using Python's time module.
3 
4 import time
5 
6 print('Press ENTER to begin, Press Ctrl + C to stop')
7 while True:
8     try:
9         input() # For ENTER. Use raw_input() if you are running python 2.x instead of input()
10         starttime = time.time()
11         print('Started')
12     except KeyboardInterrupt:
13         print('Stopped')
14         endtime = time.time()
15         print('Total Time:', round(endtime - starttime, 2),'secs')
16         break

TicTacToe.py
1 # Tic Tac Toe
2 
3 import random
4 import sys
5 
6 def get_input():
7 	if sys.version_info >= (3, 0):
8 		return input()
9 	else:
10 		return raw_input()
11 
12 def drawBoard(board):
13     # This function prints out the board that it was passed.
14 
15     # "board" is a list of 10 strings representing the board (ignore index 0)
16     print(' ' + board[7] + ' | ' + board[8] + ' | ' + board[9])
17     print('-----------')
18     print(' ' + board[4] + ' | ' + board[5] + ' | ' + board[6])
19     print('-----------')
20     print(' ' + board[1] + ' | ' + board[2] + ' | ' + board[3])
21 
22 def inputPlayerLetter():
23     # Lets the player type which letter they want to be.
24     # Returns a list with the player's letter as the first item, and the computer's letter as the second.
25     letter = ''
26     while not (letter == 'X' or letter == 'O'):
27         print('Do you want to be X or O?')
28         letter = get_input().upper()
29 
30     # the first element in the tuple is the player's letter, the second is the computer's letter.
31     if letter == 'X':
32         return ['X', 'O']
33     else:
34         return ['O', 'X']
35 
36 def whoGoesFirst():
37     # Randomly choose the player who goes first.
38     if random.randint(0, 1) == 0:
39         return 'computer'
40     else:
41         return 'player'
42 
43 def playAgain():
44     # This function returns True if the player wants to play again, otherwise it returns False.
45     print('Do you want to play again? (yes or no)')
46     return get_input().lower().startswith('y')
47 
48 def makeMove(board, letter, move):
49     if isSpaceFree(board,move):
50         board[move] = letter
51     else:
52         raise Exception("makeMove: the field is not empty!")
53 
54 def isWinner(bo, le):
55     # Given a board and a player's letter, this function returns True if that player has won.
56     # We use bo instead of board and le instead of letter so we don't have to type as much.
57     return ((bo[7] == le and bo[8] == le and bo[9] == le) or # across the top
58     (bo[4] == le and bo[5] == le and bo[6] == le) or # across the middle
59     (bo[1] == le and bo[2] == le and bo[3] == le) or # across the bottom
60     (bo[7] == le and bo[4] == le and bo[1] == le) or # down the left side
61     (bo[8] == le and bo[5] == le and bo[2] == le) or # down the middle
62     (bo[9] == le and bo[6] == le and bo[3] == le) or # down the right side
63     (bo[7] == le and bo[5] == le and bo[3] == le) or # diagonal
64     (bo[9] == le and bo[5] == le and bo[1] == le)) # diagonal
65 
66 def getBoardCopy(board):
67     # Make a duplicate of the board list and return it the duplicate.
68     dupeBoard = []
69 
70     for i in board:
71         dupeBoard.append(i)
72 
73     return dupeBoard
74 
75 def isSpaceFree(board, move):
76     # Return true if the passed move is free on the passed board.
77     return board[move].isdigit()
78 
79 def getPlayerMove(board):
80     # Let the player type in his move.
81     move = ' '
82     while move not in '1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8 9'.split() or not isSpaceFree(board, int(move)):
83         print('What is your next move? (1-9)')
84         move = get_input()
85     return int(move)
86 
87 def chooseRandomMoveFromList(board, movesList):
88     # Returns a valid move from the passed list on the passed board.
89     # Returns None if there is no valid move.
90     possibleMoves = []
91     for i in movesList:
92         if isSpaceFree(board, i):
93             possibleMoves.append(i)
94 
95     if len(possibleMoves) > 0:
96         return random.choice(possibleMoves)
97     else:
98         return None
99 
100 def getComputerMove(board, computerLetter):
101     # Given a board and the computer's letter, determine where to move and return that move.
102     if computerLetter == 'X':
103         playerLetter = 'O'
104     else:
105         playerLetter = 'X'
106 
107     # Here is our algorithm for our Tic Tac Toe AI:
108     # First, check if we can win in the next move
109     for i in range(1, 10):
110         copy = getBoardCopy(board)
111         if isSpaceFree(copy, i):
112             makeMove(copy, computerLetter, i)
113             if isWinner(copy, computerLetter):
114                 return i
115 
116     # Check if the player could win on his next move, and block them.
117     for i in range(1, 10):
118         copy = getBoardCopy(board)
119         if isSpaceFree(copy, i):
120             makeMove(copy, playerLetter, i)
121             if isWinner(copy, playerLetter):
122                 return i
123 
124     # Try to take one of the corners, if they are free.
125     move = chooseRandomMoveFromList(board, [1, 3, 7, 9])
126     if move != None:
127         return move
128 
129     # Try to take the center, if it is free.
130     if isSpaceFree(board, 5):
131         return 5
132 
133     # Move on one of the sides.
134     return chooseRandomMoveFromList(board, [2, 4, 6, 8])
135 
136 def isBoardFull(board):
137     # Return True if every space on the board has been taken. Otherwise return False.
138     for i in range(1, 10):
139         if isSpaceFree(board, i):
140             return False
141     return True
142 
143 def main():
144     print('Welcome to Tic Tac Toe!')
145     random.seed()
146     while True:
147         # Reset the board
148         theBoard = [' '] * 10
149         for i in range(9,0,-1):
150             theBoard[i] = str(i)
151         playerLetter, computerLetter = inputPlayerLetter()
152         turn = whoGoesFirst()
153         print('The ' + turn + ' will go first.')
154         gameIsPlaying = True
155     
156         while gameIsPlaying:
157             if turn == 'player':
158                 # Player's turn.
159                 drawBoard(theBoard)
160                 move = getPlayerMove(theBoard)
161                 makeMove(theBoard, playerLetter, move)
162     
163                 if isWinner(theBoard, playerLetter):
164                     drawBoard(theBoard)
165                     print('Hooray! You have won the game!')
166                     gameIsPlaying = False
167                 else:
168                     if isBoardFull(theBoard):
169                         drawBoard(theBoard)
170                         print('The game is a tie!')
171                         break
172                     else:
173                         turn = 'computer'
174     
175             else:
176                 # Computer's turn.
177                 move = getComputerMove(theBoard, computerLetter)
178                 makeMove(theBoard, computerLetter, move)
179     
180                 if isWinner(theBoard, computerLetter):
181                     drawBoard(theBoard)
182                     print('The computer has beaten you! You lose.')
183                     gameIsPlaying = False
184                 else:
185                     if isBoardFull(theBoard):
186                         drawBoard(theBoard)
187                         print('The game is a tie!')
188                         break
189                     else:
190                         turn = 'player'
191     
192         if not playAgain():
193             break
194         
195 if __name__ == "__main__":
196     main()

XOR_cipher.py
1 """
2 	author: Christian Bender
3 	date: 21.12.2017
4 	class: XORCipher
5 
6 	This class implements the XOR-cipher algorithm and provides
7 	some useful methods for encrypting and decrypting strings and
8 	files.
9 
10 	Overview about methods
11 
12 	- encrypt : list of char
13 	- decrypt : list of char
14 	- encrypt_string : str
15 	- decrypt_string : str
16 	- encrypt_file : boolean
17 	- decrypt_file : boolean
18 """
19 class XORCipher(object):
20 
21 	def __init__(self, key = 0):
22 		"""
23 			simple constructor that receives a key or uses
24 			default key = 0
25 		"""
26 
27 		#private field
28 		self.__key = key
29 
30 	def encrypt(self, content, key):
31 		"""
32 			input: 'content' of type string and 'key' of type int
33 			output: encrypted string 'content' as a list of chars
34 			if key not passed the method uses the key by the constructor.
35 			otherwise key = 1
36 		"""
37 
38 		# precondition
39 		assert (isinstance(key,int) and isinstance(content,str))
40 
41 		key = key or self.__key or 1
42 
43 		# make sure key can be any size
44 		while (key > 255):
45 			key -= 255
46 
47 		# This will be returned
48 		ans = []
49 
50 		for ch in content:
51 			ans.append(chr(ord(ch) ^ key))
52 
53 		return ans
54 
55 	def decrypt(self,content,key):
56 		"""
57 			input: 'content' of type list and 'key' of type int
58 			output: decrypted string 'content' as a list of chars
59 			if key not passed the method uses the key by the constructor.
60 			otherwise key = 1
61 		"""
62 
63 		# precondition
64 		assert (isinstance(key,int) and isinstance(content,list))
65 
66 		key = key or self.__key or 1
67 
68 		# make sure key can be any size
69 		while (key > 255):
70 			key -= 255
71 
72 		# This will be returned
73 		ans = []
74 
75 		for ch in content:
76 			ans.append(chr(ord(ch) ^ key))
77 
78 		return ans
79 
80 
81 	def encrypt_string(self,content, key = 0):
82 		"""
83 			input: 'content' of type string and 'key' of type int
84 			output: encrypted string 'content'
85 			if key not passed the method uses the key by the constructor.
86 			otherwise key = 1
87 		"""
88 
89 		# precondition
90 		assert (isinstance(key,int) and isinstance(content,str))
91 
92 		key = key or self.__key or 1
93 
94 		# make sure key can be any size
95 		while (key > 255):
96 			key -= 255
97 
98 		# This will be returned
99 		ans = ""
100 
101 		for ch in content:
102 			ans += chr(ord(ch) ^ key)
103 
104 		return ans
105 
106 	def decrypt_string(self,content,key = 0):
107 		"""
108 			input: 'content' of type string and 'key' of type int
109 			output: decrypted string 'content'
110 			if key not passed the method uses the key by the constructor.
111 			otherwise key = 1
112 		"""
113 
114 		# precondition
115 		assert (isinstance(key,int) and isinstance(content,str))
116 
117 		key = key or self.__key or 1
118 
119 		# make sure key can be any size
120 		while (key > 255):
121 			key -= 255
122 
123 		# This will be returned
124 		ans = ""
125 		
126 		for ch in content:
127 			ans += chr(ord(ch) ^ key)
128 
129 		return ans
130 
131 
132 	def encrypt_file(self, file, key = 0):
133 		"""
134 			input: filename (str) and a key (int)
135 			output: returns true if encrypt process was
136 			successful otherwise false
137 			if key not passed the method uses the key by the constructor.
138 			otherwise key = 1
139 		"""
140 
141 		#precondition
142 		assert (isinstance(file,str) and isinstance(key,int))
143 
144 		try:
145 			with open(file,"r") as fin:
146 				with open("encrypt.out","w+") as fout:
147 
148 					# actual encrypt-process
149 					for line in fin:
150 						fout.write(self.encrypt_string(line,key))
151 
152 		except:
153 			return False
154 
155 		return True
156 
157 
158 	def decrypt_file(self,file, key):
159 		"""
160 			input: filename (str) and a key (int)
161 			output: returns true if decrypt process was
162 			successful otherwise false
163 			if key not passed the method uses the key by the constructor.
164 			otherwise key = 1
165 		"""
166 
167 		#precondition
168 		assert (isinstance(file,str) and isinstance(key,int))
169 
170 		try:
171 			with open(file,"r") as fin:
172 				with open("decrypt.out","w+") as fout:
173 
174 					# actual encrypt-process
175 					for line in fin:
176 						fout.write(self.decrypt_string(line,key))
177 
178 		except:
179 			return False
180 
181 		return True
182 
183 
184

async_downloader.py
1 """
2 It's example of usage asyncio+aiohttp to downloading.
3 
4 You should install aiohttp for using:
5 (You can use virtualenv to testing)
6 
7 pip install -r /path/to/requirements.txt
8 
9 """
10 
11 import asyncio
12 import aiohttp
13 from os.path import basename
14 import concurrent.futures as cofu
15 
16 
17 def download(ways):
18 
19     if not ways:
20         print('Ways list is empty. Downloading is impossible')
21         return
22 
23     print('downloading..')
24 
25     success_files = set()
26     failure_files = set()
27 
28     event_loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
29     try:
30         event_loop.run_until_complete(
31             async_downloader(ways, event_loop, success_files, failure_files)
32         )
33     finally:
34         event_loop.close()
35 
36     print('Download complete')
37     print('-' * 100)
38 
39     if success_files:
40         print('success:')
41         for file in success_files:
42             print(file)
43 
44     if failure_files:
45         print('failure:')
46         for file in failure_files:
47             print(file)
48 
49 
50 async def async_downloader(ways, loop, success_files=set(), failure_files=set()):
51 
52     async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
53         coroutines = [
54             download_file_by_url(
55                 url,
56                 session=session,
57             ) for url in ways]
58 
59         completed, pending = await asyncio.wait(coroutines, return_when=cofu.FIRST_COMPLETED)
60         while pending:
61 
62             for task in completed:
63                 fail, url = task.result()
64 
65                 if fail:
66                     failure_files.add(url)
67                 else:
68                     success_files.add(url)
69 
70             completed, pending = await asyncio.wait(pending, return_when=cofu.FIRST_COMPLETED)
71 
72         for task in completed:
73             fail, url = task.result()
74             if fail:
75                 failure_files.add(url)
76             else:
77                 success_files.add(url)
78 
79 
80 async def download_file_by_url(url, session=None):
81 
82     fail = True
83     file_name = basename(url)
84 
85     assert session
86 
87     try:
88         async with session.get(url) as response:
89             if response.status == 404:
90                 print('\t{} from {} : Failed : {}'.format(file_name, url, '404 - Not found'))
91                 return fail, url
92 
93             if not response.status == 200:
94                 print('\t{} from {} : Failed : HTTP response {}'.format(file_name, url, response.status))
95                 return fail, url
96 
97             data = await response.read()
98 
99             with open(file_name, 'wb') as file:
100                 file.write(data)
101 
102     except asyncio.TimeoutError as err:
103         print('\t{} from {}: Failed : {}'.format(file_name, url, 'Timeout error'))
104 
105     except aiohttp.client_exceptions.ClientConnectionError as err:
106         print('\t{} from {}: Failed : {}'.format(file_name, url, 'Client connection error'))
107 
108     else:
109         print('\t{} from {} : Success'.format(file_name, url))
110         fail = False
111 
112     return fail, url
113 
114 
115 def test():
116 
117     ways = ['https://www.wikipedia.org',
118             'https://www.ya.ru',
119             'https://www.duckduckgo.com',
120             'https://www.fail-path.unknown',
121             ]
122 
123     download(ways)
124 
125 
126 if __name__ == "__main__":
127     test()

backup_automater_services.py
1 # Script Name	: backup_automater_services.py
2 # Author			: Craig Richards
3 # Created			: 24th October 2012
4 # Last Modified	: 13th February 2016
5 # Version			: 1.0.1
6 
7 # Modifications	: 1.0.1 - Tidy up the comments and syntax
8 
9 # Description		: This will go through and backup all my automator services workflows
10 
11 import datetime                         # Load the library module
12 import os                               # Load the library module
13 import shutil							# Load the library module
14 
15 today    = datetime.date.today()	    # Get Today's date
16 todaystr = today.isoformat()		    # Format it so we can use the format to create the directory
17 
18 confdir      = os.getenv("my_config")		  	   # Set the variable by getting the value from the OS setting
19 dropbox      = os.getenv("dropbox") 					 # Set the variable by getting the value from the OS setting
20 conffile     = ('services.conf') 					     # Set the variable as the name of the configuration file
21 conffilename = os.path.join(confdir, conffile) # Set the variable by combining the path and the file name
22 sourcedir    = os.path.expanduser('~/Library/Services/')	 # Source directory of where the scripts are located
23 destdir      = os.path.join(dropbox, "My_backups" + "/" +
24     "Automater_services" + todaystr + "/")   # Combine several settings to create
25 
26                                                                                     # the destination backup directory
27 for file_name in open(conffilename): 									  # Walk through the configuration file
28   fname = file_name.strip()													    # Strip out the blank lines from the configuration file
29   if fname:																			        # For the lines that are not blank
30     sourcefile = os.path.join(sourcedir, fname)		      # Get the name of the source files to backup
31     destfile = os.path.join(destdir, fname) 			      # Get the name of the destination file names
32     shutil.copytree(sourcefile, destfile)						  	# Copy the directories

batch_file_rename.py
1 # batch_file_rename.py
2 # Created: 6th August 2012
3 
4 '''
5 This will batch rename a group of files in a given directory,
6 once you pass the current and new extensions
7 '''
8 #just checking
9 __author__ = 'Craig Richards'
10 __version__ = '1.0'
11 
12 import os
13 import argparse
14 
15 def batch_rename(work_dir, old_ext, new_ext):
16     '''
17     This will batch rename a group of files in a given directory,
18     once you pass the current and new extensions
19     '''
20     # files = os.listdir(work_dir)
21     for filename in os.listdir(work_dir):
22         # Get the file extension
23         split_file = os.path.splitext(filename)
24         file_ext = split_file[1]
25         # Start of the logic to check the file extensions, if old_ext = file_ext
26         if old_ext == file_ext:
27             # Returns changed name of the file with new extention
28             newfile = split_file[0] + new_ext 
29 
30             # Write the files
31             os.rename(
32                 os.path.join(work_dir, filename),
33                 os.path.join(work_dir, newfile)
34             )
35 
36 def get_parser():
37     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='change extension of files in a working directory')
38     parser.add_argument('work_dir', metavar='WORK_DIR', type=str, nargs=1, help='the directory where to change extension')
39     parser.add_argument('old_ext', metavar='OLD_EXT', type=str, nargs=1, help='old extension')
40     parser.add_argument('new_ext', metavar='NEW_EXT', type=str, nargs=1, help='new extension')
41     return parser
42 
43 def main():
44     '''
45     This will be called if the script is directly invoked.
46     '''
47     # adding command line argument
48     parser = get_parser()
49     args = vars(parser.parse_args())
50 
51     # Set the variable work_dir with the first argument passed
52     work_dir = args['work_dir'][0]
53     # Set the variable old_ext with the second argument passed
54     old_ext = args['old_ext'][0]
55     if old_ext[0] != '.':
56         old_ext = '.' + old_ext
57     # Set the variable new_ext with the third argument passed
58     new_ext = args['new_ext'][0]
59     if new_ext[0] != '.':
60         new_ext = '.' + new_ext
61 
62     batch_rename(work_dir, old_ext, new_ext)
63 
64 
65 if __name__ == '__main__':
66     main()
